    *   **Missing Control:** The paper lacks a direct comparison with a "pulse-level" simulation. The authors use a gradient-scaling approximation for Non-Linear Write (NL), which is a significant simplification of the actual stochastic pulse programming process.
*   **Energy Estimation:**
    *   The energy model absorbs interconnect and routing overhead into SRAM costs. This is a first-order approximation that likely underestimates the true energy cost, potentially inflating the claimed 11.45x gain.

### **4. Presentation & Narrative**
*   **Narrative Arc:** The story is clear: Problem (lack of organic-specific simulators) → Solution (Profile-driven framework) → Findings (Instance overfitting is the main issue, not quantization) → Impact (Ensemble HAT fixes it).
*   **Abstract:** The abstract accurately reflects the results, highlighting the Ensemble HAT breakthrough.
*   **Length & Figures:** The length seems appropriate for NC. Figures are generally clear, but **Figure 1** relies heavily on stylized artwork which is standard, but the energy breakdown (**Figure 5**) is crucial and well-placed.
*   **Over-explained:** The Related Work section is comprehensive but standard for hardware papers. The discussion on "Scale Masking" is insightful and necessary.

### **5. Missing References or Comparisons**
*   **Missing Comparisons:**
    *   **Analog ViT Deployments:** The paper should compare against recent digital/analog hybrid ViT deployments on *inorganic* CIM (e.g., works on RRAM or FeFET crossbars) to better contextualize the "11.45x" energy gain.
    *   **Optical Frontends:** While organic devices are compared, a reference to the broader literature on "Optical Neural Networks" (ONNs) or "In-Sensor Computing" using CMOS image sensors might provide a stronger baseline for the optical frontend discussion.
*   **Citations:** The reference list is extensive, but ensure inclusion of the latest 2025/2026 works on *analog* vision transformers specifically (beyond just quantization papers).

### **6. Specific Issues**
*   **Line 145 (Main Text):** "We treat the framework as a first-order behavioral simulator rather than a routed-chip emulator."
    *   *Comment:* This disclaimer is good, but it needs to be reinforced in the Energy section where the gains look deceptively high.
*   **Line 285 (Main Text):** "The strongest positive result is that Ensemble HAT raises fresh-instance Tiny-ViT accuracy from 10.00% to 86.37 ± 1.54%."
    *   *Comment:* This is a dramatic claim. Ensure the supplementary methods clearly explain why standard HAT fails so catastrophically (10% is random chance) while Ensemble HAT works.
*   **Line 325 (Main Text):** "The observed NL = 2.0 failure boundary... should be interpreted as the limit of this first-order approximation."
    *   *Comment:* This is a caveat. The authors are essentially saying the model breaks when the physics gets too complex, which is fine, but it limits the "hard boundary" claim.
*   **Table 2 (Main Text):** The standard deviation for the "ConvNeXt-Tiny V3" is missing in the CIFAR-10 column in the text provided. Statistical significance must be uniform.
*   **Supp Line 1.3.3:** The sensitivity analysis uses a "compact 2D sweep."
    *   *Comment:* Clarify if this was done via actual retraining or just inference-time simulation. If the latter, it doesn't prove the training robustness.

### **7. Questions for Authors**
1.  **Calibration Overhead:** Your energy model assumes "ideal calibrated digital rescaling." In real organic CIM arrays, how significant is the overhead of the calibration circuitry (ADC/DAC for read-write loops) required to achieve this "ideal" state? Could this overhead negate the energy gains for small/tiny edge vision models?
2.  **Non-Linear Write Approximation:** You model non-linear write dynamics (NL) as a gradient scaling factor during backpropagation. How does this correlate with the actual stochastic pulse-width modulation required to program organic devices? Is there a risk that the "hard boundary" of NL=2.0 is an artifact of the simulation method rather than a physical limit?
3.  **Instance Overfitting:** The collapse to 10% accuracy on fresh D2D instances is severe. Is this a known phenomenon in organic devices, or is it specific to the Transformer architecture due to the softmax attention mechanism? Can you provide intuition on why CNNs (ResNet) don't suffer as much from this "instance overfitting"?

### **8. Overall Recommendation**
**Major Revision**

**Justification:**
The manuscript presents a timely and well-structured simulation framework that addresses a genuine gap in evaluating organic neuromorphic hardware for modern vision tasks. The findings regarding "hardware-instance overfitting" and the proposed "Ensemble HAT" solution are insightful and valuable for the community. However, the paper currently overstates its energy efficiency claims by neglecting the routing and calibration overhead inherent in "first-order" models. Furthermore, the validation of the non-linear write model remains purely algorithmic. To meet *Nature Communications* standards, the authors must temper their claims regarding energy gains, provide a more rigorous justification for their non-linear write approximation, and better contextualize their results against inorganic CIM baselines.

## hunyuan

### 1. Summary  
This manuscript presents a profile-driven, first-order behavioral simulation framework for organic optoelectronic compute-in-memory (CIM) inference, targeting edge vision applications. The core claim is that quantization alone is not the dominant bottleneck in organic CIM deployment; instead, hardware-instance transferability, nonlinear write dynamics, and peripheral constraints (e.g., ADC precision) critically limit performance. The framework bridges material-level device characterization (via literature-derived profiles) to system-level vision tasks (CIFAR-10/100, Flowers-102) using ResNet-18, ConvNeXt-Tiny, and Tiny-ViT-5M backbones, demonstrating that Ensemble Hardware-Aware Training (HAT) mitigates fresh-instance collapse (raising accuracy from 10.00% to 86.37±1.54%) but severe nonlinear write remains a hard boundary (27.72±0.82%).  


### 2. Significance & Novelty  
- **Gap Addressed**: The work fills a critical gap in organic CIM research, where existing simulators (e.g., AIHWKIT, CrossSim, NeuroSim) focus on inorganic memories and lack support for organic-specific challenges (optical frontends, state-dependent noise, profile substitution). It addresses the "materials-to-system" decision gap for edge vision deployment.  
- **Contribution Type**: Primarily methodological, with experimental validation via simulation. Key innovations include: (1) a PyTorch-based framework integrating organic device non-idealities (nonlinear write, proportional noise, retention) and optical frontend effects; (2) a "profile-driven" interface for seamless literature-to-simulation parameter substitution; (3) extension of robustness analysis to modern vision transformers (Tiny-ViT-5M) and ensemble HAT strategies.  
- **Comparison to Existing Frameworks**: Unlike inorganic-focused tools (e.g., NeuroSim’s circuit-level detail, CrossSim’s parasitic modeling), this framework prioritizes organic-specific physics (optoelectronic tuning, shot noise amplification) and hybrid analog/digital deployment for transformers. It complements rather than replaces mature inorganic simulators.  
- **Impact for NC Readers**: Highly relevant to the CIM/neuromorphic hardware community. The focus on organic devices—an emerging area for low-power edge vision—and the framework’s transparency in linking device profiles to system performance align with NC’s scope of interdisciplinary innovation. The work is NC-level but requires clarification of simulation limitations to avoid overstati

## sonar

This is a comprehensive read of both the main paper and supplementary material. I now have enough detail to write a thorough review. Let me compose it.

# Reviewer #2 Report — *Nature Communications*

**Manuscript:** "Hardware-Aware Simulation of Organic Optoelectronic Compute-in-Memory Inference for Edge Vision"
**Author:** Songqiao Li
**Submitted:** April 10, 2026

***

## 1. Summary

This manuscript presents a PyTorch-based, profile-driven behavioral simulation framework for evaluating organic optoelectronic compute-in-memory (CIM) inference applied to edge vision tasks. The core claim is that the framework bridges the gap between materials-level device characterization (conductance range, C2C/D2D noise, retention, write nonlinearity) and task-level accuracy and energy trends for modern vision backbones — specifically Tiny-ViT-5M, ResNet-18, and ConvNeXt-Tiny evaluated on CIFAR-10/100 and Flowers-102. The paper's headline results include: Ensemble HAT raising fresh-instance accuracy from 10.00% to 86.37 ± 1.54%, a Zhang 2026 OPECT profile case study reaching 88.53%, and severe nonlinear write remaining a hard boundary at 27.72 ± 0.82%. The paper is explicitly positioned not as a chip-predictive emulator but as a "transparent materials-to-system decision bridge". [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/2146c06f-fa6e-45ec-b23d-798d87fe528a/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=hooD7H79L2ghjQajMZJ0B3OP0nc%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

***

## 2. Significance & Novelty

### Genuine Gap Addressed

The paper correctly identifies a real and underserved gap: existing CIM simulators (NeuroSim, AIHWKIT, CrossSim, MemTorch) are calibrated around inorganic resistive memories and do not natively support organic-specific phenomena — optoelectronic frontend distortion, profile substitution for arbitrary technologies, or hybrid Transformer deployment under organic-device constraints. The problem statement is well-motivated, and the decision to test on Tiny-ViT-5M — a contemporary hybrid Transformer — is a meaningful step beyond the small-perceptron benchmarks typical in organic-neuromorphic literature. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/2146c06f-fa6e-45ec-b23d-798d87fe528a/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=hooD7H79L2ghjQajMZJ0B3OP0nc%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

### Contribution Type

The contribution is primarily **methodological and software-architectural** rather than experimental. There are no new device fabrication results; all device parameters are literature-derived or analytically assumed proxy values. The paper is transparent about this, which is commendable. However, it significantly limits the novelty of the physical claims. The "profile-driven" interface is architecturally sensible, but its core idea — injecting parameterized noise into a PyTorch forward pass — is not fundamentally new relative to AIHWKIT or MemTorch. The differentiation comes from *specialization to organic devices and ViT hybrid mapping*, which is real but incremental. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

### Comparison to Existing Frameworks

The paper does compare itself to AIHWKIT, CrossSim, NeuroSim, and MemTorch, and the supplementary provides a bounded sanity-check comparison against an AIHWKIT analog-tile proxy (96.88% digital vs. 91.80 ± 1.02% AIHWKIT analog, matched regime). However, **this comparison is limited to a 256-sample test subset of ResNet-18/CIFAR-10**. There is no quantitative crosswalk on retention fidelity, write-nonlinearity modeling, or multi-seed accuracy distributions. The statement "the present simulator and a mature inorganic toolkit exhibit the same qualitative degradation trend" is too weak to serve as a validation claim. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

### Venue Suitability

This is a borderline case for *Nature Communications*. NC publishes high-impact multidisciplinary work where the novelty is clear and the experimental evidence is strong. This manuscript is a well-executed systems simulation study with honest limitations, but **it lacks experimental hardware validation**, and its novelty over existing frameworks is incremental rather than transformative. The paper would be a stronger fit for venues such as *npj Computational Materials*, *IEEE Transactions on Electron Devices*, *Frontiers in Neuroscience (Neuromorphic Engineering)*, or *ACM Transactions on Architecture and Code Optimization*. If the authors can supplement with even preliminary measured-device validation against the profile predictions, the case for NC strengthens considerably.

***

## 3. Technical Soundness

### Simulation Assumptions

The behavioral modeling choices are generally reasonable for a first-order framework. Gaussian D2D (fixed per chip) and C2C (resampled per forward pass) noise, double-exponential retention anchored to DNTT transients (τ₁ = 140 ms, τ₂ = 610 ms, A₀ = 0.6 from Vincze et al. 2026), and STE-based gradient scaling for write nonlinearity are all standard or defensible approximations. The supplementary is admirably detailed in listing parameter provenance and explicitly flagging proxy estimates. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

**However, several assumptions raise concerns:**

- **Differential-pair symmetry assumption:** The framework assumes that positive and negative branches share identical transfer characteristics apart from sampled stochastic perturbations. For organic OECTs, systematic asymmetry arising from ionic migration history, contact variability, and gate-electrolyte coupling is known to be significant and correlated across devices. This is acknowledged in limitations but is not stress-tested. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)
- **Retention model scope:** The state-dependent vs. uniform retention comparison (Table S5) shows <0.1 pp difference. However, this validation is scoped exclusively to the Ensemble HAT V4 checkpoint — i.e., the most robust checkpoint in the study. The authors themselves note they did not replicate the comparison on the collapsing standard-HAT or non-HAT paths. The conclusion that "uniform decay sufficiency is validated" is therefore *regime-specific* and should not be generalized in the main text without this caveat. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)
- **Nonlinear write modeling:** The NL LTP/NL LTD implementation is a gradient-scaling approximation, not a pulse-faithful physical model. The NL = 2.0 failure boundary (27.72 ± 0.82%) is the limit of this approximation, not a fundamental materials constraint. This is stated honestly, but the *interpretation* of the result needs care: readers may incorrectly conclude that severe write nonlinearity is categorically fatal for organic-CIM ViT inference, when in reality the failure may partly reflect the coarseness of the STE scaling rule. ### Device-to-System Mapping

The differential conductance mapping (weight → G⁺ − G⁻ over [G_min, G_max], quantized to n_states levels with STE) is correctly formulated and clearly described. Scale recovery is modeled as ideal calibrated digital post-processing, and the paper is transparent that its control overhead is not separately costed. **This is a significant idealization.** In real crossbar inference, scale recovery requires either on-chip calibration hardware (ADC reference, digital correction, LUT lookup) or off-chip re-calibration passes, all of which consume energy and introduce latency. The energy model therefore underestimates total peripheral cost in a way that may be non-trivial. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/2146c06f-fa6e-45ec-b23d-798d87fe528a/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=hooD7H79L2ghjQajMZJ0B3OP0nc%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

### Statistical Rigor

- The multi-seed campaign is incomplete at time of submission. The paper presents a "rerun sanity check" for V4 (single seed-42 rerun: 88.45% clean, 87.64 ± 0.48% noisy MC over 10 runs) rather than the planned multi-seed summary. This is a notable gap: the canonical results are anchored to a limited seed set, and the final multi-seed statistics are explicitly described as "still being accumulated". - Monte Carlo evaluation uses 10 forward passes for most claims, which is adequate for mean estimation at the reported precision (±0.5 pp) but may underestimate tail risk for rare catastrophic failure modes.
- The ConvNeXt proportional-noise HAT result is described inconsistently: "91.98% in the best single run" versus "84.75 ± 0.72%" over three seeds. The three-seed result is appropriately labeled as indicating "favorable-stochastic-basin sensitivity," but reporting both numbers without clarifying which appears in the summary Table 2 creates ambiguity. - The sensitivity sweep in Table S3 shows numerically identical rows across all C2C values at fixed D2D. While the interpretation (D2D dominates, C2C is sub-resolution) is physically plausible, **identical entries across a sweep warrant explicit explanation** in the main text — a reader encountering this table without the supplementary text would reasonably suspect a formatting error. ### ADC and Energy Modeling

- The "6-bit knee" observation (∼27% accuracy at 4-bit ADC, >80% at 6-bit) is a noteworthy and practically important result. However, the ADC model uses "behavioral DNL/INL modeling"  without specifying the DNL/INL magnitude assumptions or whether they correspond to measured organic-peripheral circuits or generic CMOS ADC specs. This matters because organic or hybrid ADCs may have substantially worse DNL. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/2146c06f-fa6e-45ec-b23d-798d87fe528a/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=hooD7H79L2ghjQajMZJ0B3OP0nc%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)
- The energy estimate (273.94 µJ per inference, 11.45× reduction vs. FP32) is explicitly labeled as a "first-order, upper-bound-like estimate". The routing overhead sensitivity analysis (adding 10–50% overhead reduces gain from 11.45× to 9.90–11.10×) is helpful. However, the FP32 reference energy (3.14 mJ, derived from 2.5 pJ per MAC × op count) is a very rough estimate; the actual MAC energy depends heavily on the target platform and precision. The comparison should cite a specific hardware platform or use a range of reference values. ***

## 4. Presentation & Narrative

### Story Arc

The four-question structure (quantization bottleneck → task complexity → instance transfer → physical stress limits) is a logical and effective organizing principle. The story arc from problem to findings is generally clear, and the honest self-positioning as a "decision bridge rather than chip emulator" is a mature and credible framing that sets appropriate expectations. ### Abstract Quality

The abstract is largely accurate and well-written. It correctly emphasizes the headline results (Ensemble HAT: 10.00% → 86.37 ± 1.54%; nonlinear write boundary: 27.72 ± 0.82%) and the "first-order upper-bound" caveat for energy. However, the statement "distribution-matched proportional-noise retraining can recover to 97.37 ± 0.05%" is potentially misleading without the qualification that this result holds only under the *same* noise regime and does not transfer to uniform noise — a critical nuance buried in Section 6.2. ### Figures

The figures are generally appropriate. Notable issues:

- **Figure 1 (stack diagram):** The caption notes that "detailed operator semantics are described in the caption, not embedded in the figure," and the figure itself contains a box labeled "Behavioral abstraction used for all simulator experiments / Detailed operator semantics are described in the caption, not embedded in the figure" — this is meta-text that should not appear inside the figure. This suggests the figure was not finalized for submission.
- **Figure 5 (energy breakdown):** The "Buffer" entry is labeled "not modeled", which is fine to acknowledge, but it appears as an empty bar in what is presented as a complete energy breakdown. This should be footnoted more prominently. ### Length and Format

The paper is well-structured for NC format. The main text is approximately 13 pages with 7 sections, which is appropriate. The supplementary (∼10 pages) is detailed and honest. No major sections feel rushed or unnecessarily padded.

***

## 5. Missing References & Comparisons

The reference list is adequate but has several notable gaps:

- **MemTorch validation studies:** MemTorch  is cited as a related framework, but no published MemTorch accuracy benchmarks on CNN/ViT tasks are directly compared against the present results. Even a qualitative table showing "this framework vs. MemTorch vs. AIHWKIT under matched assumptions" would greatly strengthen the positioning.
- **Analog ViT inference literature:** There is growing literature on analog/in-memory computing for Vision Transformers specifically (e.g., Hersche et al., IBM analog ViT studies, PIM-ViT proposals). The related work section in Section 2.2 mentions "ViT-on-PIM studies" without citing specific papers — this gap should be filled.
- **Organic CIM accuracy benchmarks:** The closest prior work on variability-aware organic network mapping is the Alibart et al. perceptron study , which is correctly cited. However, no accuracy number from that work is given for comparison, even qualitatively. A brief quantitative anchor (e.g., "Alibart et al. demonstrated X% on Y-class task") would help contextualize the CIFAR-scale advance. - **Flowers-102 failure analysis:** The complete failure of HAT on Flowers-102 for ConvNeXt is treated as a hypothesis ("data starvation") without citing low-data fine-tuning literature that might provide comparative context for this failure mode.

6. **[Section 5.3, retention plateau claim]:** The paper states retention "validates uniform decay sufficiency" based on <0.1 pp differences, but this validation is only on the Ensemble HAT checkpoint. The corrected V4 retention (Supplementary Fig. S4) actually shows a **severe drop from 91.63% to 82.66% at 1 s**, then a plateau near 79%. The main text should explicitly state this degradation magnitude — it is a significant practical limitation that is currently understated. ### Moderate Issues

7. **[Section 3.2]:** The STE-based nonlinear write surrogate is described, but the exact functional form of the gradient scaling factor is deferred to the supplementary. For a methodology-focused paper, this derivation should appear in the main text or at minimum in a dedicated equation box.

8. **[Section 5.8, FP32 energy reference]:** The 2.5 pJ/MAC assumption for FP32 energy (yielding 3.14 mJ reference) is from Horowitz 2014, now 12 years old. Modern GPU/edge accelerators have substantially different per-MAC energy profiles. A more current reference or a range of platform-specific estimates is needed. 9. **[Section 6.4, "analog ceiling" discussion]:** The observation that digital attention (QK^T, softmax) accounts for 57.9% of hybrid inference energy is important. However, the claim that "INT8 ViT deployments on digital accelerators consume 2.0–4.0 mJ per inference"  is presented without citation. Reference  (I-ViT) should be explicitly cited here, or the number removed. 10. **[Section 1.3.2, Vincze 2026 accessibility]:** The supplementary states "Vincze et al. may not be uniformly accessible during review", which implies it may be a preprint or early-access paper. If so, the retention parameters — which underpin the entire canonical organic profile — rest on a not-yet-peer-reviewed source. The authors should clarify the publication status and consider whether alternative anchoring is needed. ### Minor Issues

11. **[Abstract]:** "any energy advantage... should be read as a first-order, upper-bound-like estimate rather than a routed chip measurement" — this phrasing is correct in spirit but awkward. Consider: "energy estimates are upper-bound projections from an analytical model and should not be interpreted as routed-circuit measurements."

12. **[Section 2.2]:** MemTorch is described as demonstrating "memristive non-idealities embedded into PyTorch workflows"  — this is accurate, but the sentence implies MemTorch is purely about inference. MemTorch also supports training simulation; this distinction matters when comparing scope. ## 7. Questions for Authors

1. **Multi-seed completeness:** The paper acknowledges that the "full multi-seed campaign is still being accumulated". When will this data be available? The current submission appears to rest on a rerun sanity check (one seed) rather than the intended multi-seed summary. Should resubmission be contingent on completing this campaign? [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

2. **Validation against physical hardware:** The framework's defining promise is that "the same protocol can later be rerun with measured JSON profiles in place of the current literature-anchored priors". Is there any plan or timeline for such validation? Without at least one instance of a predicted vs. measured accuracy comparison, the profile-driven methodology remains unverified. What would constitute a minimal validation experiment? [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

3. **6-bit ADC knee interpretation:** The sharp accuracy transition at 6-bit ADC is attributed to readout precision dominating over weight noise. However, the ADC model uses behavioral DNL/INL modeling — what specific DNL/INL values were assumed, and are these representative of organic or hybrid CMOS ADCs that would realistically accompany an organic crossbar? [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/2146c06f-fa6e-45ec-b23d-798d87fe528a/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=hooD7H79L2ghjQajMZJ0B3OP0nc%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

4. **Ensemble HAT generalization:** The Ensemble HAT strategy (resampling D2D masks each epoch) improves fresh-instance accuracy at a "∼1.00× wall-clock overhead". This seems to imply negligible computational overhead, which is surprising. How is this overhead measured, and does it account for the additional forward passes required per epoch? What is the expected overhead for larger models or longer training schedules? 5. **Differential-pair asymmetry:** The framework assumes equal transfer characteristics for positive and negative conductance branches apart from stochastic perturbations. For OECTs with electrochemical gating, the LTP and LTD pathways are physically distinct (cation insertion vs. expulsion), and systematic branch asymmetry is expected. How sensitive are the headline results to a systematic branch offset of, say, 5–10% of the conductance window? ***

## 8. Overall Recommendation

**Recommendation: Major Revision**

This manuscript addresses a genuine and underserved problem — providing a deployment-facing simulation framework specifically tailored to organic optoelectronic CIM — and does so with commendable transparency about its limitations. The four-question experimental structure is well-conceived, the supplementary is unusually thorough in tracking parameter provenance, and the honest self-positioning as a "decision bridge rather than chip emulator" reflects scientific maturity. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/2146c06f-fa6e-45ec-b23d-798d87fe528a/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=hooD7H79L2ghjQajMZJ0B3OP0nc%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

However, several issues prevent acceptance in the current form. First, the multi-seed statistical campaign is incomplete, and some key results (e.g., the ConvNeXt proportional-noise HAT number) are inconsistently reported between the best-single-run and multi-seed values. Second, there are concrete numerical inconsistencies between the abstract, Table 1, and Table 2 that must be resolved. Third, the framework comparison against AIHWKIT and CrossSim is limited to a 256-sample sanity check that does not constitute a rigorous crosswalk. Fourth, the retention-model validation is scoped only to the most robust checkpoint, and the main text understates the severity of the V4 retention drop (from ~91% to ~79% at 1 s). Fifth, the figure body contains production-level meta-text indicating the manuscript is not yet in final form. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/c3c8e763-b475-461b-b758-e335e1515f0b/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYEZ4AX7LZM&Signature=PdFJLWOyxYfmaRPRw8MR4MJOB04%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJIMEYCIQD6xbkaOwXYzMJfhPal4GG6lLz6iCPLFTsqjuI5fYe44wIhAPnYOUcagxewI1qmgZENLNTyw638Yy%2BtvMC09j4LEKdCKvMECDEQARoMNjk5NzUzMzA5NzA1IgwXDiNCRAkevTzfOLEq0ATW9g3ri1W5MuzDJECszC01Ler2wPOp3yBsj%2Br8grhvk1XsiOS%2BPVIuBQodPv%2FeNfnLe1hyuT3MNusvtMRQiGcZA9iBy8%2FFq4sPj1LItOAPv4wqpDBPcME6dnwHlDELlMLa3yab%2BXDyOVUqlBK2U0OmcmMW7l%2FusM5nHu67rs6IfyJM4gjy70AArgIbvcPZ6kGu0otW911xYt7hyJJGIPCjGMvl38iUwP1Ke550y1zBi7bpsqZvbYUyQnNLEXf0nmWtQKSJKzXKacedMQDJbvTvuhAaTDrQwJD0glZ3FNydvBqGrkZQivD%2FjjkE517P3vNWnvUqYkL39WrmcYAgf8pHg0KxGKM4ulLFWHqyBPQR1f%2FGt9Olz1OX5lLxjNsZTSCBxPmLdWktmrl0Nz2tkE6WisySgzCrkE%2B2eikkkzSJO7agwkpCvSNY8mb%2F48iJbDf3xd8FxqsAwJ1DGfEXhSrUuOZQ81chwGCFK5wsR43%2Fv%2FzdRo8OP8HP25kT8DhosDxiJfGpUI6ttvDjb5raGPlW6QGpBm0EKKrvq53b7thF9PTIMVhvcHt8nuMKnQpeH8%2BGuucYlUqnEd1BVBnppspgMXmr3qebJionB5ib6PO%2FbqbxC7DDrRc7ec66IkrzTi%2B3i24OVD4nkyVsA7iD898fz1t4PGQ%2F1HAQM56iVrL5HJI8xeUCruab2UPd6dqz9wX%2BYv6tc5wNDV3J9sXi%2FrFS1lArFYOOm0IWCR4XAjYpnuSF3lv3NNeIdRUtdAAYh3%2Bl76DP%2FeNwpxfDtl8m5uNPMLm75M4GOpcBeQt8IbbvELYHA51hiyPkfRJkC97aKBjsoDU1iLvOFsbQ6IQmIlcTdPdhGH711rztMVAXBPZonLkA5RpQnGy2sefDJyylDgIXl8M93QMzPmvErmvKnTL8CCgnLjAy3jFPNIud1aE%2FO%2B462OEscCoT77D8EUlWqNdD34B5aQfLh1AQlqgIjPUUULLGMGyz6lpGzayikZwvAw%3D%3D&Expires=1775837931)

If the authors can complete the multi-seed campaign, resolve the numerical inconsistencies, sharpen the framework comparison (even with a compact matched-regime accuracy table against MemTorch or AIHWKIT), and adequately qualify the scope of the retention and proportional-noise validation claims, this work has merit for publication. The target venue question remains open: the present simulation-only contribution may be better positioned at *npj Computational Materials* or *IEEE Transactions on Electron Devices* unless hardware validation data can be added to support NC-level impact. The authors should address this question explicitly in their revision letter.

## nemotron

### 1. Summary  

The manuscript presents a **profile-driven**, PyTorch-integrated behavioral simulator that maps literature-derived or measured organic optoelectronic synaptic device characteristics (conductance range, variability, retention, nonlinear write, photoresponse) to task-level accuracy and energy for hybrid analog/digital edge-vision inference.  The core claim is that for Tiny-ViT, ConvNeXt-Tiny, and ResNet-18 backbones on CIFAR-10/100 and Flowers-102, nominal quantization and standard uniform variability are often not the dominant deployment bottlenecks once scale recovery and hardware-aware training (HAT) are enabled; instead ADC precision, task complexity, fresh hardware instances, and richer device physics dominate failure modes.  The work further claims that an Ensemble HAT scheme can dramatically improve hardware-instance robustness (Tiny-ViT fresh-instance accuracy from 10.00% to 86.37 ± 1.54%) and that the same simulator can ingest a literature-derived organic OPECT profile to yield deployment-facing predictions (88.53% with Zhang 2026 profile).  Energy modeling suggests an 11.45× upper-bound energy reduction for hybrid Tiny‑ViT relative to an FP32 digital baseline, with clear caveats that this is a first-order estimate, not a routed-chip result.  Overall, the paper positions the framework as a transparent “materials-to-system decision bridge” rather than a chip-predictive emulator. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/784d984c-ba65-4de4-9ab2-ea220b6d5a93/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=NjyI%2FfCqzqoUGlFmmkHfGfN9F1E%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)

***

### 2. Significance & Novelty  

The work targets an important gap between device-level characterization of organic optoelectronic synaptic devices and realistic system-level deployment analysis for modern vision models, which is indeed underexplored compared to inorganic ReRAM/PCM-focused simulators.  Conceptually, the key novelty is not the idea of analog CIM simulation itself (well established by DNN+NeuroSim, MemTorch, AIHWKIT, CrossSim) but: (i) a profile-substitution interface explicitly tailored to organic optoelectronic devices, (ii) inclusion of an optoelectronic frontend model (photoresponse + inverse-gamma compensation), and (iii) the focus on hybrid ViT deployment with hardware-aware training and multi-instance Ensemble HAT.  The contribution is primarily methodological (framework design, modeling abstractions and training protocols) with substantial experimental work on multiple backbones and datasets; there is no new device fabrication but the simulation matrix is broad and reasonably systematic.  Relative to AIHWKIT, CrossSim, and NeuroSim-like frameworks, the main differentiators are: explicit organic parameter provenance, hooked JSON profile interface, integrated retention and optical-frontend modeling, and the Ensemble HAT fresh-instance treatment; however, the paper currently underplays a more direct, quantitative comparison against these simulators beyond a single small AIHWKIT sanity check in the Supplementary. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/891a6500-501d-4bf0-98be-04f8a54d7bb6/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=bMO%2Fw0GmHmdLb8GBO8BSOnHy%2F20%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)

From a Nature Communications perspective, the topic (organic CIM for edge vision, ViT-centric hardware-aware simulation, materials-to-system bridge) is aligned with the journal’s neuromorphic and device+system readership, and the work is clearly more substantial than a narrow ML paper.  However, because the study is entirely simulation-based and many modeling choices are deliberately first-order, the NC-level impact hinges on convincing the reader that: (a) the simulation fidelity is sufficient to meaningfully inform materials and architecture decisions, and (b) the framework is genuinely generalizable beyond the particular parameter choices and tasks explored. At present, these aspects are promising but not fully demonstrated; I would consider this potentially NC-suitable after a fairly extensive major revision that strengthens validation, comparative analysis, and clarity around claims. ***

### 3. Technical Soundness  

**Simulation assumptions & physical justification**  
The paper is commendably explicit about which physical effects are modeled (differential-pair mapping, Gaussian D2D/C2C variability, double-exponential retention, nonlinear write surrogates, ADC/DAC energy and distortion, photoresponse nonlinearity) and which important effects are excluded (IR drop, sneak paths, temperature dependence, spatial optical crosstalk, detailed layout asymmetry, pulse-faithful programming).  The device parameters for the canonical organic profile and Zhang 2026 OPECT case study are carefully tabulated with provenance and explicit labels for proxy assumptions; this is a strong point.  At the same time, several simplifying assumptions are quite aggressive for analog hardware prediction: (i) perfect common-mode cancellation in differential pairs apart from sampled variability; (ii) uniform retention being “validated” only on a single regime (V4 Ensemble HAT on CIFAR-10) and then used more broadly; (iii) Gaussian, uncorrelated noise for D2D/C2C, with no spatial correlation or input-dependent parasitics.  The authors do repeatedly emphasize that the model is “first-order,” but some of the conclusions edge toward being more general than the justified scope unless carefully rephrased. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/784d984c-ba65-4de4-9ab2-ea220b6d5a93/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=NjyI%2FfCqzqoUGlFmmkHfGfN9F1E%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)

**Device-to-system mapping**  
The mapping from FP32 weights to bounded conductance [Gmin, Gmax] via differential pairs, quantization to nstates, and reconstruction of effective weights is standard and reasonably described in both main text and Supplementary.  The treatment of D2D as a fixed Gaussian offset per device and C2C as per-forward Gaussian noise, optionally proportioportional to |G|, is conventional; the retention model \(G(t)=G_0[A_0 e^{-t/\tau_1} + (1-A_0)e^{-t/\tau_2}]\) anchored to Vincze is also standard for organic devices.  [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/784d984c-ba65-4de4-9ab2-ea220b6d5a93/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=NjyI%2FfCqzqoUGlFmmkHfGfN9F1E%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108) However, the “nonlinear write” is implemented as a simple gradient-scaling factor within the STE rather than as explicit pulsed write dynamics, which means that the reported severe NL = 2.0 failure at 27.72 ± 0.82% is more a statement about the chosen training surrogate than about real physical programming limits (the authors admit this, but it is not consistently highlighted when that result is used as a “hard boundary”).  [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/891a6500-501d-4bf0-98be-04f8a54d7bb6/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=bMO%2Fw0GmHmdLb8GBO8BSOnHy%2F20%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)  

Similarly, the “scale masking” phenomenon—where scale recovery plus 4-bit quantization largely hides uniform noise—is plausible but depends strongly on assumed calibration (ideal layer-wise scale recovery, perfect digital rescaling) and error-free ADC/DAC transfer of those scales.  Because the ADC distortions are only behaviorally modeled and not fully detailed in the main text, it is hard to judge whether the 6-bit “cliff” is robust across more realistic converter impairments. **Experimental controls, ablations, and seeds**  
The experimental protocol is relatively thorough:  

- Multiple architectures (ResNet‑18, ConvNeXt‑Tiny, Tiny‑ViT‑5M) and datasets (CIFAR‑10, CIFAR‑100, Flowers‑102). Nonetheless, there are some shortcomings for a journal like NC:  

- Some key claims (e.g., retention plateau and sufficiency of uniform retention; ADC bit-width “knee” at 6 bits; energy breakdown and 11.45× gain; proportional noise vs uniform) depend on single-configuration sweeps with limited seeds. - Ensemble HAT is only lightly characterized: the impact of number of instances, resampling schedule, and capacity-robustness trade-off is discussed qualitatively but not systematically ablated. - For ConvNeXt proportional-noise HAT, the text notes a single best run at 91.98% but then emphasizes 84.75 ± 0.72% over three seeds, highlighting favorable-basin sensitivity; by contrast, some other regimes are reported with fewer robustness checks. **Statistical reporting**  
The authors frequently report mean ± standard deviation for noisy forward passes and sometimes across seeds, which is good practice.  The supplementary sensitivity sweep for Zhang OPECT shows 95% confidence intervals and interprets apparently identical rows as stability rather than copy-paste, which is a nice touch.  However, not all reported results include error bars (e.g., some ADC sweep points, some energy estimates, some digital baselines).  For NC, it would be helpful to standardize reporting (e.g., always MC over at least 5–10 noisy runs and 3 seeds for each regime, particularly for the headline results like 86.37 ± 1.54% fresh-instance accuracy). **Quantization, noise injection, retention, ADC, energy modeling**  

- Quantization: 4-bit weight quantization with STE is standard; but activation quantization and attention-related dynamic ranges are not described in enough detail for ViT, especially given known sensitivities in Q-ViT/FQ-ViT. - Noise injection: Gaussian, independent per-device noise is a reasonable starting point, but the paper sometimes interprets regime-specific findings (e.g., limited C2C impact vs D2D dominance for a particular checkpoint) as more general than they are; this should be more explicitly caveated as “for this profile and model.” [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/784d984c-ba65-4de4-9ab2-ea220b6d5a93/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=NjyI%2FfCqzqoUGlFmmkHfGfN9F1E%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)
- Retention: Only one case (Ensemble HAT V4 on CIFAR-10) is used to justify that uniform retention is sufficient, comparing to a state-dependent model where high-conductance states decay 20% faster; the observed <0.1 pp difference in accuracy is specific to that regime and cannot support broader conclusions about retention modeling sufficiency. - ADC modeling: The main text identifies a 6-bit accuracy cliff and attributes it to ADC resolution, but details of INL/DNL modeling, noise, and pipeline quantization are largely confined to Supplementary and remain high-level; this should be more transparent, as this conclusion is central to the “analog ceiling” discussion. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/784d984c-ba65-4de4-9ab2-ea220b6d5a93/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=NjyI%2FfCqzqoUGlFmmkHfGfN9F1E%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)
- Energy estimation: The analytical model is clearly first-order (MAC energy, ADC/DAC per element, digital ops, SRAM traffic) with routing absorbed into memory terms, and the authors even sweep hypothetical extra routing overheads (10–50%) to show that the 11.45× gain degrades only modestly.  This is reasonable for a simulation paper, but the claim “11.45× lower than FP32” should consistently be framed as “upper-bound estimate” in all places, including the abstract and key figures, to avoid implying chip-level measurement. Overall, the technical framework is coherent and reasonably grounded for a simulation study, but some of the bolder verbal conclusions should be narrowed to match the actual scope of the modeling assumptions and limited validation against existing simulators or hardware.  

***

### 4. Presentation & Narrative  

The story arc—gap between organic-device characterization and system-level viability; introduction of a profile-driven simulator; exploration of four deployment-facing questions; results around quantization vs converters vs instance transfer vs richer physics; and concluding on an “analog ceiling” and Ensemble HAT—is clear and logically laid out.  The abstract does a good job of explicitly marking the simulator as “first-order behavioral” and of signaling that energy figures are upper-bound-like, though the phrase “should therefore be read as a first-order, upper-bound-like estimate rather than a routed chip measurement” appears only late in the abstract and could be foregrounded earlier. Some issues:  

- The paper is on the long side for NC, particularly given that it is purely simulation-based; certain narrative sections (Discussion 6.x) are quite wordy and repeat points already made, which could be tightened. - The separation between “canonical” regimes and “physical extension” regimes (proportional noise, NL=2, Ensemble HAT, optical frontend) is somewhat buried; highlighting this taxonomy earlier (with a concise table of experiment families) would clarify the story. In general, the manuscript is well written, with good use of signposting and explicit “core value conclusion” statements; only modest tightening and rebalancing between main text and Supplementary are needed.  

***

### 5. Missing References or Comparisons  

The paper already cites key CIM-simulation references (DNN+NeuroSim, MemTorch, AIHWKIT, CrossSim) and an extensive set of organic neuromorphic and optoelectronic synapse works, including recent OPECT arrays and in-sensor computing architectures that bound realistic device parameters.  The connection to ViT quantization literature (post-training and training-aware Q-ViT, FQ-ViT) is also acknowledged. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/784d984c-ba65-4de4-9ab2-ea220b6d5a93/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=NjyI%2FfCqzqoUGlFmmkHfGfN9F1E%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)

However, for NC-level rigor, I see a few gaps:  

- More direct comparison with AIHWKIT and CrossSim: The Supplementary includes a single ResNet-18/CIFAR-10 sanity check where an AIHWKIT analog tile achieves 91.80 ± 1.02% versus a digital baseline of 96.88%, used to argue that the present simulator exhibits “the same qualitative degradation trend” under one matched regime.  This is quite thin. A more systematic alignment (e.g., multiple regimes, inclusion of retention/drift modeling in CrossSim, calibration of noise parameters) would substantially strengthen claims of correctness for the behavioral model. [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/784d984c-ba65-4de4-9ab2-ea220b6d5a93/supplementary_main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=NjyI%2FfCqzqoUGlFmmkHfGfN9F1E%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)
- Additional recent ViT-on-PIM / ViT-on-CIM works: The paper cites works on ReRAM-based ViT accelerators and workload orchestration, but there are likely more recent edge-ViT hardware-aware studies (including in-memory attention engines) that could be cited to contextualize the decision to keep QK⊤ and Softmax digital and to quantify the “analog ceiling.” [ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws](https://ppl-ai-file-upload.s3.amazonaws.com/web/direct-files/attachments/158931923/891a6500-501d-4bf0-98be-04f8a54d7bb6/main.pdf?AWSAccessKeyId=ASIA2F3EMEYE5EAXOR6Q&Signature=bMO%2Fw0GmHmdLb8GBO8BSOnHy%2F20%3D&x-amz-security-token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEGgaCXVzLWVhc3QtMSJGMEQCICx6e59aRYRtiwvtnpYPBkgsXcXgwSapM6hSo%2BAOjwigAiA8P57gQ8FYtmlkYUmrni5iAZjv0kcTRT%2Bbuf1hcZzu3yrzBAgxEAEaDDY5OTc1MzMwOTcwNSIM1SoNYtiyZTvVY7g0KtAEmRhYGzDaAPFSSRzAuUrSL%2B2GpOZtmEsq1tu5SUgKCePNxjXaldesjbq8nm4Xhmfyw5qkjxYhIDWv1ljGBdAFq157nxGfPAR2Mr7DwI6FaoOFzQyFt798ZpC8KRC9alcT0cdGmVHOkIb6xdVQL%2BmlygNcmNLxyV%2FN9cgvXexkjs%2FQoq%2Fj0s1zwOvFTi%2FbtukhzO7hA303%2BlQEVqQjmSztVRTQ6OG6vmCZN2dzbl6RhOjg9nZsZEOSuviqc8%2Bv2uQd9wj6N5%2Bjdz8Poqe4Wy17w7dYciqhHnkjwsy1DvTst6Q%2Bfm0i67Nkbx8EDGHnkQEJmjoQM4qeXEoMcRDdvmaJMM6h2agQ9gzZqIq9E%2F1XN%2BMGPgqpdqdWIe6e4iiZBuxwvS7g6CzkfZhgM%2BWHG5rT2Dn3eieXW91PixM4d2%2FQM9%2BZSxzXRivHP6MWL26Ruoy%2Ff3HNwOs%2B8kVtWtXEnC2HtglWFJuZU2QwxVrEUe3bRk%2Bi654q%2BDj0KVrmsKuzVgxRo2gwnAjriW6gTHfIC49vj63Ns3GZe9dKw3%2Fbw9arCaEmtMWQ0fedkl%2B5qddD2ueD2Ki4m0JYUICkHIV8Vbc0xOGrGRQuWL3qOb%2BdFPf49dDp6a968LPFijLh%2BvM5vZUP3dCjlJNQT%2FpuYjUDX4xXemMtmJtOQjCzdnmJqDiYRigF%2F7GwbblVRUke7vvfanaWXiS7z9RCC7wYfJThj15THJMvHBZFPdUY%2F9jysztMlg17CdMU8trwzt6yIUwiJjmYMOUCA9UoGE7Z7PmmrTK%2B%2FTC3vuTOBjqZAQTN9g1B%2BqkeScM%2FIMvKlm1SQ8JL1aTp%2BmJTXnPPuBQT1uzKHU9f6254jWPrErwW%2BcQVFxLaMnfvYuvIHlU%2BUn4GRgwUbAFmfoDQgcYUlTEY82M6z01HKM8rZY2Qw2VcB7%2BR%2Bg8ZLk9fDMz5ZTWk%2BSxSOH3pmQqcumtmHwnsjOuEzawbqxU8Cw56hMjmNF3YJJXjMvpZHH1ATg%3D%3D&Expires=1775838108)
- Organic CIM / synaptic transistor modeling works: While device-level organic synapse references are numerous, explicit prior art on simulation-level organic CIM (beyond the Alibart Monte Carlo perceptron) is relatively lightly discussed; if there are any recent works that couple organic synaptic arrays to CNNs/ViTs via behavioral models, they should be compared. Also, the Discussion cites estimated IR-drop-induced accuracy degradations of 1–3% based on ReRAM benchmarks; this relies on external works and could benefit from explicit reference to those specific IR-drop modeling studies (some are in the reference list but not clearly tied to the numerical claim).
